main()
{

	scanf("%d",&b);

	printf("%d\ +\ %d\ =\ %d\n",a,b,a+b);
	printf("%d\ -\ %d\ =\ %d\n",a,b,a-b);
	printf("%d\ *\ %d\ =\ %d\n",a,b,a*b);
	printf("%d\ /\ %d\ =\ %d",a,b,a/b);
}

#include"stdio.h"
main()
{
	float a,s,b;
	scanf("%f",&a);
	if(a>0)
	{
	s=a/1;
	b=a/1+1;
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	printf("%d\n",(int)s);
    }
	if(a<0)
	{
	s=a/1;
	b=a/1-1;
	printf("%d\n",(int)s);
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	}
	if(a==0)
	{
	printf("0");
    }

20190318063:Problem1240:正确
#include"stdio.h"
main()
{
	char t;
	scanf("%c",&t);
	if((t>='A')&&(t<='T'))
	{
	t+=6;
	printf("%c\n",t);
	}
	if(t=='U')
	{
	printf("A");
    }
    if(t=='V')
	{
	printf("B");
    }	
	if(t=='W')
	{
	printf("C");
    }	
	if(t=='X')
	{
	printf("D");
    }	
	if(t=='Y')
	{
	printf("E");
    }	
	if(t=='Z')
	{
	printf("F");
    }
}

	a=x+y;
	b=x-y;
	c=x*y;
	d=x/y;
	printf("%d+%d=%d\n",x,y,a);
	printf("%d-%d=%d\n",x,y,b);
	printf("%d*%d=%d\n",x,y,c);
	printf("%d/%d=%d\n",x,y,d);
}

20190301017:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);
}

    for (int i = 1; i < 4; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < i; j++)
        {
            printf("  %.2f ", a);
        }
        printf("\b\n");
    }
    return 0;
}
------------------------------------------------------

#include<stdio.h>
#include<math.h>
int main()
{
	int a,b,c,d,e,f;
	scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
	c=a+b;
	d=a-b;
	e=a*b;
	f=a/b;
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n%d - %d = %d\n%d * %d = %d\n%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,c,a,b,d,a,b,e,a,b,f);
	return 0;
}

	c=(int)a;
	i=0;
	while(i<=c)
	{
		i=i+1;
		d=i;
	}
	printf("%d\n",d);
	printf("%d\n",c);
}

20190301012:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);
}

{

    printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,a-b);
    printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,a*b);
    printf("%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,a/b);
    return 0;
}

int main(void)
{
    char a, b;
    a = getchar();
    b = a + 6;
    if ('Z' <= b)
    {
        b = a + 6 + 'A' - 'Z' - 1;
    }
    printf("%c", b);
    return 0;
}

#include<math.h>
main()
{
	float a,b,c;
	scanf("%f",&a);
	
	for(b=0; b<3;b++);
	{
		for(c=0;c<b+1;c++);
		{
			printf("%6.2f\n",a);
			printf("%6.2f %6.2f\n",a,a);
			printf("%6.2f %6.2f %6.2f\n",a,a,a);
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
    return 0;
}

20190301026:Problem1024:答案错误
#include <stdio.h>

int main ()
{//先实验，是不是整数只有1-9 .不是。
//还有10级100，跨站至1000 
	//10-99 2    ;100-999 3 
	double a;
	int x,y,z,l,m; 
	scanf("%lf",&a);
	printf("%d\n",(int)((a-((int)a))/0.1));
	
	l=(int)a;//假设整数部分为小于1000的数 
	if((l>=0)&&(l<=9)) printf("%d\n",l);
	if((l>=10)&&(l<=99)) {
	
	x=l/10;
	
	l=l-x*10;
	printf("%d\n",l); 
}
	if((l>=100)&&(l<=999)){
	
	x=l/100,y=(l-100*x)/10,l=l-x*100-y*10;
	printf("%d\n",l);
}
	if((l>=1000)&&(l<=9999)){
		
		x=l/1000,y=(l-x*1000)/100,z=(l-x*1000-y*100)/10,l=l-1000*x-100*y-10*z;
		printf("%d\n",l);
	}
	return 0;
}

#include <stdio.h>
int main()
{
    int firstNumber, secondNumber, sumOfTwoNumbers;
    
    printf("输入两个数(以空格分割): ");
 
    // 通过 scanf() 函数接收用户输入的两个整数
    scanf("%d#%d", &firstNumber, &secondNumber);
 
    // 两个数字相加
    sumOfTwoNumbers = firstNumber + secondNumber;
 
    // 输出结果
    printf("%d",sumOfTwoNumbers);
 
    return 0;
}

main()
{

	c = a + b;
	p = a - b;
	m = a * b;
	n = a / b;
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,c);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,p);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,m);
	printf("%d / %d = %d",a,b,n);
}

int main()
{
  float a, i, j;
  scanf("%f", &a);

  for (i = 1; i <= 3; i++)
  {
    for (j = 1; j <= i; j++) 
    {
      printf("%6.2f ", a);
    }
    printf("\n");
  }
}

int main(void)
{
	int a,b,c,d,e,f;
	scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
	c=a+b;
	d=a-b;
	e=a*b;
	f=a/b;
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,c);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,d);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,e);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,f);
	return 0;
}

20190318089:Problem1024:正确
#include"stdio.h"
int main()
{
	float a,b,c;
	scanf("%f",&a);
	if(a>0)
	{
	b=a+1;
	c=a;
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	printf("%d\n",(int)c);
	}
	if(a<0)
	{
	b=a;
	c=a-1;
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	printf("%d\n",(int)c);
	}
	if(a==0)
	{
	printf("0");
	}
}

20190318066:Problem1060:正确
#include<stdio.h>
 
int main()
{
	
	float n, i, j;
	 
	scanf("%f",&n);
	
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
	return 0;
}

#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	int n,m,sum,j,c,cf;
	scanf("%d%d",&n,&m);
	sum=n+m;
	j=n-m;
	c=m*n;
	cf=n/m;
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",n,m,sum);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",n,m,j);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",n,m,c);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n",n,m,cf);
 }

#include<math.h>

    int a,b;
    double c;
    scanf("%lf",&c);
    a=floor(c);
    b=ceil(c);
    printf("%d\n",b);
    printf("%d\n",a);
    return 0;
}

20190318016:Problem1024:答案错误
//小数的上限和下限
#include "stdio.h"
#include "math.h"
main()
{
	int b,c;
	double a;
	scanf("%f\n",a);
	b=floor(a);//floor函数是<=a的整数
	c=ceil(a);//ceil函数是>=a的整数
	printf("%d\n",c);
	printf("%d\n",b); 
 }

20190318075:Problem1060:正确
#include<stdio.h> 
int main()
{
	float n, i, j;
	scanf("%f",&n);
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
	return 0;
}

20193621020:Problem1024:答案错误
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <math.h>
#include <string.h>

int main()
{
    char s[100];
    int i;
    gets(s);
    for(i=0;i<100;i++)
    {
        if(s[i]=='.')
        {
            printf("%d\n",strlen(s)-1-i);
            printf("%d\n",i);
        }
    }
}

#include<stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>

int main()
{
	int x, y;
	int a, b, c;
	double d;
	scanf("%d%d",&x,&y);
	a = x + y;
	b = x - y;
	c = x * y;
	d = x / y;
	printf("%d+%d=%d\n",x,y,a);
	printf("%d-%d=%d\n",x,y,b);
	printf("%d*%d=%d\n",x,y,c);
	printf("%d/%d=%lf\n",x,y,d);
	
	return 0;

}

	printf("%d-%d=%d\n",x,y,b);
	printf("%d*%d=%d\n",x,y,c);
	printf("%d/%d=%d\n",x,y,d);

#include "stdio.h"
#include "math.h"
main()
{
	float x;
	scanf("%f",&x);
	x=((float)(int)((x+0.005)*100))/100;//保留两位小数 
	printf("%6.2f\n",x);
	printf("%6.2f %6.2f\n",x,x);
	printf("%6.2f %6.2f %6.2f\n",x,x,x);
}

20190318018:Problem1238:正确
#include"stdio.h"
main()
{
	int a,b,c,d,e,f;
	scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
	c=a+b;
	d=a-b;
	e=a*b;
	f=a/b;
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,c);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,d);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,e);
	printf("%d / %d = %d",a,b,f);
}

20190318163:Problem1238:正确
#include<stdio.h>

int main(void)
{
	int m,n;
	scanf("%d %d",&m,&n);
	
	int A,B,C,D;
	A=m+n;
	B=m-n;
	C=m*n;
	D=m/n;
	
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",m,n,A);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",m,n,B);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",m,n,C);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n",m,n,D);
	
	return 0;
}

/*这是用ASC吗转换英文字母的代码。*/
#include"stdio.h"
main()
{
	char a;
	int b;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	b=(int)a;
	if (b+6<90&&b>=65)
	printf("%c\n",(char)b+6);
	else
	printf("%c\n",(char)b-20);
}

main()
{
	int a,b;
	scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,a+b);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,a-b);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,a*b);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,a/b);
}

int main(void)
{
	char a,b;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	
	if(a + 6 > 'Z')
    {
    	b='A'+5+a-'Z';
    	printf("%c",b);
	}
	else(a + 6 < 'Z');
	{
		b = a + 6;
		printf("%c",b);
	}
	return 0;
}

20190301004:Problem1060:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	float n, i, j;
	scanf("%f",&n);
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
}

{
	char a; // int
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if ( a >= 'A' && a <= 'Z' )  {
		a = a + 6;
		if ( a > 'Z') {
			a = a - 26; // a -= 26;
		}
	}
	printf("%c", a);
}

20190318124:Problem1060:答案错误
#include "stdio.h"
main()
{
	float n;
	scanf("%d",&n);
	for(int i=1;i<4;i++)
	{
		for(int j=1;j<=1;j++)
		{
			if(j==i)
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			else
			printf("%6.2f",n);
		}
		printf("\n");
    }
    return 0;
}

main()   
   {
	char a,b,c,d;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a+6<=90){
	
	printf("%c",a+6);
}
	if(a+6>90){
	
	c=90-a;
	d=6-c-1;
	b=65+d;
	printf("%c",b);
}
  }

20190318017:Problem1240:正确
void main() {
    char n;      //声明变量。
    scanf("%c",&n);
    n += 6;
    if(n>90)
    {
    	n-=26;
	}
	n = (char)n;      //输出强转为char类型的变量（即该字母的ASCII码值）。
    printf("%c", n);
    printf("\n");
}

20190318135:Problem1060:正确
#include<stdio.h>
 
int main()
{
	
	float n, i, j;
	 
	scanf("%f",&n);
	
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
	return 0;
}

20190301011:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);
}

20190301018:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);
}

void main() {
    char n;      //声明变量。
    scanf("%c",&n);
    n += 6;
    if(n>90)
    {
    	n-=26;
	}
	n = (char)n;      //输出强转为char类型的变量（即该字母的ASCII码值）。
    printf("%c", n);
    printf("\n");
}

	printf("%d+%d = %d\n",a,b,c);
	printf("%d-%d = %d\n",a,b,d);
	printf("%d %d = %d\n",a,b,e);
	printf("%d/%d = %d\n",a,b,f);
}

int main ()

int a，b，c，d，x，y;
 scanf（“%d%d”，&a，&b）;
c=a+b；
d=a-b；
x=a*b；
y=a/b；
printf("%d\%d\n%d\n%d\n.，c，d，x，y")；
return 0；
｝

int main（）
｛
int a，b;
scanf("%d %d",&a，&b);
printf("%d + %d = %d\n"，a，b，a+b)；
printf(“%d - %d = %d\n”，a，b，a-b);

20190318002:Problem1238:正确
#include<stdio.h>
#include<math.h>
int main()
{
	int a,b;
	scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,a+b);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,a-b);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,a*b);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,a/b);
}

main()
{
	int x, y;
	scanf("%d %d", &x, &y);
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n", x, y, x + y);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n", x, y, x - y);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n", x, y, x * y);
	printf("%d / %d = %d\n", x, y, x / y);
}

}

{

   if(a+6<91)
   b=a+6;

   b=a+6-90+64;//-90指多出的字母数，+64指从A又开始数！

    float i;

    scanf("%f", &i);

    printf("  %6.2f\n", i);

    printf("  %6.2f   %6.2f\n", i, i);

    printf("  %6.2f   %6.2f   %6.2f\n", i, i, i);

    return 0;

}

{

	printf("%d + %d = %d \n", a , b , a + b );
	printf("%d - %d = %d \n", a , b , a - b );
	printf("%d * %d = %d \n", a , b , a * b );
	printf("%d / %d = %d \n", a , b , a / b );
}

{

    int A,B,C,D;
    A=m+n;
    B=m-n；
    C=m*n；
    D=m/n;
    printf("%d+%d=%d\n",m,n,A);
    printf("%d-%d=%d\n",m,m,B);
    printf("%d*%d=%d\n",m,n,C);
    printf("%d/%d=%d\n",m,n,D);
    return 0;

int main(void)
{
	int a, b;
	scanf("%d%d", &a, &b); 
	printf("%d + %d = %d\n", a, b, a + b);
	printf("%d - %d = %d\n", a, b, a - b);
	printf("%d * %d = %d\n", a, b, a * b);
	printf("%d / %d = %d", a, b, a / b);
	return 0;
}

20190318088:Problem1060:正确
#include<stdio.h> 
int main()
{
	float n, i, j;
	scanf("%f",&n);
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
	return 0;
}

{
    double a;
    int b;

    b=(int)a;
    if(a>=0)
    {
        printf("%d\n",b+1);
        printf("%d",b);
    }
    if(a<0)
    {
        printf("%d\n",b);
        printf("%d",b-1);
    }
}

/*输入一个大写英文字母。
输出这个大写英文字母加6后所等到的大写英文字母。若加6时超过了‘Z’则回到‘A’算起。*/
#include <stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a='x',b='y';
	scanf("%c",&a);
	b=a+6;
	if(b<=90)
	printf("%c\n",b);
	else

20190301023:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);
}

20190301040:Problem1024:正确
/*输入一个小数（double类型）
输出2行，第一行为该小数的天花板，第二行为该小数的地板，请注意最后行尾输出换行。
不用考虑整数溢出的问题。*/
#include <stdio.h>
#include <math.h>
main()
{
	int a,b;
	double c;
	scanf("%lf",&c);
	b=floor(c);
	a=ceil(c);
	printf("%d\n",a);
	printf("%d\n",b);
}

20190318164:Problem1238:正确
#include<stdio.h>
  
int main()
{
int a,b;
scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
  
int A,B,C,D;
A=a+b;
B=a-b;
C=a*b;
D=a/b;
  
printf("%d + %d = %d\n",a,b,A);
printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,B);
printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,C);
printf("%d / %d = %d\n",a,b,D);
  
return 0;
}

	}
	else {
		s=a-20;
		printf("%c\n,s");
	}
}

20190301034:Problem1240:正确
#include "stdio.h"
main()
{
	int n;
	char op,oc;
	scanf("%c",&op);
	while(op>='A'&&op<='Z')
	{
		oc=op+6;
		if(oc>'Z')
		{
			n='Z'-op;
			oc='A'+(6-n-1);
		}
		printf("%c",oc);
		break;
	}
}

int main()
{
	float n, i, j;
	scanf("%f",&n);
	for(i=0; i<3; i++)
	{
		for(j=0;j<i+1;j++)
		{
			printf("%6.2f",n);
			printf(" ");
		}
		printf("\n");
	}
	return 0;
}

20190301027:Problem1240:正确
#include<stdio.h>
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if(a=='U')
		printf("A\n");
	if(a=='v')
		printf("B\n");
	if(a=='W')
		printf("C\n");
	if(a=='X')
		printf("D\n");
	if(a=='Y')
		printf("E\n");
	if(a=='Z')
		printf("F\n");
	if(a!='U'&&a!='V'&&a!='W'&&a!='X'&&a!='Y'&&a!='Z')
		printf("%c\n",a+6);

			printf("%6.2f",n);

		}

    scanf("%d %d",&a,&b);
    c=a+b;
    printf("%d+%d=%d\n",a,b,a+b);
    d=a-b;
    printf("%d-%d=%d\n",a,b,a-b);
    e=a*b;
    printf("%d*%d=%d\n",a,b,a*b);
    f=a/b;
    printf("%d/%d=%d\n",a,b,a/b);
    return 0;
}

main()
{
	float a,s,b;
	scanf("%f",&a);
	if (a>0)
	{
	s=a/1;
	b=a/1+1;
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	printf("%d\n",(int)s);
	}
	if(a<0)
	{
	s=a/1;
	b=a/1-1;
	printf("%d\n",(int)s);
	printf("%d\n",(int)b);
	}
	if(a==0)
	{
		printf("0");
	}
}

    f=a/b;

    printf("%d-%d=%d\n",a,b,d);
    printf("%d*%d=%d\n",a,b,e);
    printf("%d/%d=%d\n",a,b,f);
    return 0;
    
}

20190302017:Problem1240:正确
#include"stdio.h"
main()
{
	char a;
	scanf("%c",&a);
	if (a>='A'&& a<='Z'){
		a=a+6;
		if (a>'Z'){
			a=a-26;
		}
	}
	printf("%c",a);
}

    printf("%d - %d = %d\n",a,b,a-b);
    printf("%d * %d = %d\n",a,b,a*b);
